**Question:** How did Sri Rama set out for Ayodhya along with all his people?

**Answer:** Vibhishana offered the Pushpaka Vimana, which could reach Ayodhya in one day. Rama agreed, and after bidding farewell to Sugriva and others, they all boarded the Vimana and departed for Ayodhya.

**Key entities:** Rama, Ayodhya, Vibhishana, Sugriva

#### Q5

**Question:** How did Sri Rama converse with Sita while traveling on the Pushpaka?

**Answer:** Rama pointed out to Sita various landmarks: Lanka, the battlefield, Mandodari mourning, the sea and the bridge, Madhuvana, Pampa, Kishkindha, Rishyamuka mountain, the banyan tree where Jatayu lived, the hermitages of sages like Sharabhanga, the Ganges, and Shringaberipura. Sita suggested bringing Sugriva's women to Ayodhya, and Rama agreed.

**Key entities:** Rama, Sita, Lanka, Mandodari, Kishkindha, Rishyamuka, Jatayu, Ganga, Sugriva, Ayodhya

### Chapter 99: Ninety-ninth Chapter

- Kanda: Yuddha Kanda
- Sarga range: 127-131
- Source PDF pages: 245, 246, 247
- Printed page numbers: 249, 250, 251
- Key entities: Rama, Hanuman, Bharata, Sita, Agastya, Vishvamitra, Sugriva, Vibhishana, Angada, Shatrughna, Jabali, Indra
- Places: Ayodhya

**Summary:** Rama lands the Pushpaka Vimana three yojanas from Ayodhya and enters the hermitage of Sage Bharadvaja. After accepting hospitality, he sends Hanuman ahead to Bharata. Hanuman informs Bharata of Rama's return, and Bharata joyfully prepares for Rama's coronation. The chapter describes the grand welcome and the coronation ceremony of Rama and Sita.

#### Q1

**Question:** At a distance of three yojanas from Ayodhya, after landing the Pushpaka Vimana, which great sage's hermitage did Sri Rama enter?

**Options:**
- 1. Sage Agastya
- 2. Sage Bharadvaja
- 3. Sage Vasishtha
- 4. Sage Vishvamitra

**Correct answer:** Sage Bharadvaja

**Key entities:** Ayodhya, Rama

#### Q2

**Question:** After accepting the hospitality arranged by the sage in the hermitage, whom did Sri Rama first send to Bharata?

**Options:**
- 1. Sugriva
- 2. Vibhishana
- 3. Hanuman
- 4. Angada

**Correct answer:** Hanuman

**Key entities:** Rama, Bharata, Hanuman

#### Q3

**Question:** Who first told Bharata the history of Sri Rama's exile?

**Answer:** Hanuman

**Key entities:** Bharata, Rama, Hanuman

#### Q4

**Question:** How did Bharata organize the welcome arrangements and coronation efforts for Sri Rama?

**Answer:** As soon as he heard Hanuman's words, Bharata joyfully looked at Shatrughna and said, 'Brother! Our elder brother, Lord Ramachandra, is coming here by dawn. Decorate the city of Ayodhya beautifully this very night.' As soon as he commanded, the citizens of Ayodhya decorated the city beautifully by the early morning of that day. Then, as dawn broke, the queen mothers, preceptors, ministers, army chiefs, city leaders, soldiers holding flags and banners, along with priests, people of various professions, holding flower garlands and sweet items, with Vasishtha and others following, Bharata, delighted at the auspicious arrival of Sri Ramachandra, bowed his head to the Lord's sandals and waited with royal honors. Then, at a distance, the divine Pushpaka Vimana was seen. As the Vimana descended close to them, everyone there saw Lord Ramachandra in the Vimana. Then Bharata approached Sri Rama and said, 'Brother! Accepting our mother's words, I now return to you this kingdom that you gave me as a trust. Therefore, O Lord! Be crowned king of this kingdom and rule us, your devotees and servants. May the whole world be filled with joy seeing your coronation festival.' To Bharata's words, Sri Rama said, 'So be it!' Then Bharata assigned the necessary arrangements for the coronation to each person according to their duty.

**Key entities:** Bharata, Rama, Hanuman, Shatrughna, Ayodhya

#### Q5

**Question:** How did Sri Rama's coronation take place?

**Answer:** After everyone reached Ayodhya in a procession from Nandigrama, they decorated the platform with the jeweled throne for Rama's coronation in every way. Ministers, all government officials, and city leaders who came to witness the coronation sat in seats appropriate to their status. Then the family priest Sri Vasishtha, amidst the chanting of Vedic mantras by the ritvijas, seated the fully ornamented Sri Sita and Ramachandra on the jeweled throne. Then, with auspicious musical instruments and Vedic mantras, Vasishtha, Vamadeva, Jabali, and other great sages anointed Lord Ramachandra, the supreme being, with pure fragrant waters, as the Vasus anointed Indra. Then, with Vedic mantras, they anointed Sita and Rama with holy waters mixed with various herbal essences. Then, following the lineage, the jeweled crown that Manu first wore at his coronation and that all lords of Ayodhya had worn, Sri Vasishtha Maharshi placed on the head of Ramachandra seated on the jeweled throne, with Vedic mantras. Then the ritvijas also adorned the Lord with other ornaments. Thereafter, Lord Ramachandra became emperor, made Bharata the crown prince, performed many sacrifices like the Ashvamedha, and ruled the kingdom for many years, looking after the people like his own children.

**Key entities:** Rama, Ayodhya, Sita, Jabali, Indra, Bharata
